### Post by drpjkurian on 2015-06-10
I feel this message might be from LM sensors which senses the temperature
see the [link1]("https://bugs.debian.org/cgi-bin/bugreport.cgi?bug=485674")
[link2]("http://www.wilderssecurity.com/threads/what-is-your-system-temprature.304848/")
